# Orbit traces of odd numbers under 1000

Here is the same table printed 3 times:
- in order of ascending n 
- sorted by stopping distance, to group numbers with similar fates 
- sorted by orbit (backwards), to show where they merge

Many adjacent odd numbers have the same stopping time, but diverge for (usually 3 or 6) steps before joining. The intermediate steps are often strongly correlated (part of a chain of almost-doublings).

# `n`          a positive odd integer
# `base2`      the binary representation of n
# `base3`      the ternary representation of n
# `factors`    the prime factors of n
# `dist`       the number of odd-to-odd Collatz for n steps to reach 1
# `nl`         the odd core valuation of the even number to the left of odd n
# `ocldist`    the Collatz odd-to-odd distance of the odd core of n-1
# `nr`         the odd core valuation of the even number to the right of odd n
# `ocrdist`    the Collatz odd-to-odd distance of the odd core of n+1
# `orbit_back` the remaining orbit of n under the odd-to-odd Collatz map, bacwards from 1

n,   base2,      base3,   factors,   dist, nl,      ocldist, nr,      ocrdist, orbit_back
